game.modding.terminal.echo("\n | You are hosting: SAW (Starblast Asteroid War)\n");

//  --------- NE SONT PAS ADAPTé AUX PARTIES AVEC PLUS DE 2 TEAMS ---------

//  --------- EXPERIMENTAL ---------

var GameCommandsHues = this.customOptions.hues;
st = function(who) {
  if (game.findShip(who).team === 1) {
    game.findShip(who).set({team:0,hue:GameCommandsHues[0]});
    game.modding.terminal.echo("\n | "+game.findShip(who).name+" has switched to: orange\n");
  } else {
    game.findShip(who).set({team:1,hue:GameCommandsHues[1]});
    game.modding.terminal.echo("\n | "+game.findShip(who).name+" has switched to: light blue\n");
  }
};

//  ---------- ---------- ----------

var starting_ship = this.customOptions.starting_ship;
var spectator_ship = this.customOptions.spectator_ship;
sp = function(who) {
  let hue;
  if (game.findShip(who).team === 0) {
    hue = GameCommandsHues[0];
  } else {
    hue = GameCommandsHues[1];
  }
  if (game.findShip(who).type === spectator_ship) {
    game.findShip(who).custom.SpectatingTheGame = false;
    game.findShip(who).set({type:game.findShip(who).custom.oldship,collider:true,idle:false,shield:999,stats:game.findShip(who).custom.oldstats,crystals:game.findShip(who).custom.oldcrystals,hue:hue});
    game.modding.terminal.echo("\n | "+game.findShip(who).name+" is not spectating the game anymore\n");
  } else {
    game.findShip(who).custom.oldship = game.findShip(who).type;
    game.findShip(who).custom.oldcrystals = game.findShip(who).crystals;
    game.findShip(who).custom.oldstats = game.findShip(who).stats;
    game.findShip(who).custom.SpectatingTheGame = true;
    game.findShip(who).set({type:spectator_ship,hue:280,collider:false,stats:77777777});
    game.modding.terminal.echo("\n | "+game.findShip(who).name+" is now spectating the game\n");
  }
};

game.modding.commands.players = function(){
  game.modding.terminal.echo(" | Total amount of players: "+game.ships.length);
  game.modding.terminal.echo("\n | List of players and their IDs:\n");
  for (let i=0; i<game.ships.length; i++){
    if (game.ships[i].team === 1) {team = "light blue"}
    else {team = "orange"}
    game.modding.terminal.echo(" | ID: "+game.ships[i].id+", Name: "+game.ships[i].name+", Type: "+game.ships[i].type+", Team: "+team); 
  }
  game.modding.terminal.echo("\n");
};

sac = function(who) {
  if (game.findShip(who).custom.AdmCommandsGiven !== true) {
    game.findShip(who).setUIComponent(Adm_Button);
    game.modding.terminal.echo("\n | "+game.findShip(who).name+" now has acces to the Admin Pannel\n");
    game.findShip(who).custom.AdmCommandsGiven = true;
  } else {
    game.findShip(who).setUIComponent({id:"adm_button",visible:false});
    game.findShip(who).custom.AdmCommandsGiven = false;
    game.findShip(who).custom.Adm_Windon_open = false;
    game.modding.terminal.echo("\n | Removed acces of the Admin Pannel to "+game.findShip(who).name+"\n");
    game.findShip(who).setUIComponent({id:"window",visible:false});
    game.findShip(who).setUIComponent({id:"clear_all",visible:false});
    game.findShip(who).setUIComponent({id:"spectate",visible:false});
    game.findShip(who).setUIComponent({id:"change_gamestep",visible:false});
  }
};

//  --------- --------- --------- --------- --------- --------- ---------

var bg = function(ship,vtf) {
  ship.setUIComponent({id: "Background",position: [-5,-5,110,110],clickable: false,visible: vtf,
    components: [
      {type:"box",position:[0,0,100,100],fill:"rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.15)",stroke:"#FF0000"},
      {type: "text", position: [0,9,100,7], color: "rgb(55,255,255)", value: "SAW (Starblast Asteroid War)"}
    ]
  });
};

game.modding.commands.pause = function() {
  for (let ship of game.ships) {
    bg(ship,true);
    ship.set({collider:false,idle:true,vx:0,vy:0});
    AddText(ship,"Game paused","rgb(55,255,55)");
    clearTimeout(this.ptm);
  }
  OldNextWaveTimer = NextWaveTimer;
  NextWaveTimer = 0.001;
  game.modding.terminal.echo("\n | Game paused.\n");
};

game.modding.commands.play = function() {
  for (let ship of game.ships) {
    bg(ship,false);
    if (ship.type === spectator_ship) {ship.set({idle:false})} 
    else {ship.set({collider:true,idle:false})}
    AddText(ship,"Game resumed...","rgb(55,255,55)");
    this.ptm = setTimeout(() => {ship.setUIComponent({id:"Text",visible: false})}, 5000); // jshint ignore:line
  }
  gs(OldNextWaveTimer);
  game.modding.terminal.echo("\n | Game resumed.\n");
};

lg = function(yn) {
  restartall = function() {
    for (let ship of game.ships) {
      ship.setUIComponent({id:"Text",visible: false});
      ship.setUIComponent({id:"NextWaveTimer",visible: false});
    }
  };
  if (!yn) {
    restartall();
    NextWaveTimer = -2;
    Time = 100*60;
    game.modding.terminal.echo("\n | Game started, waiting time: "+(Time/60)+" minutes.\n");
  } else {
    Time = 5;
    NextWaveTimer = -2;
    restartall();
    game.modding.terminal.echo("\n | Game will be starting in: "+Time+" seconds.\n");
  }
};

gs = function(step,addtime) {
  for (let ship of game.ships) {
    ship.setUIComponent({id:"Text",visible: false});
    ship.setUIComponent({id:"NextWaveTimer",visible: false});
    ship.setUIComponent({id:"BackgroundStart",visible: false});
  }
  NextWaveTimer = step;
  if (addtime >= 0) {
    Time = addtime*60;
  }
  game.modding.terminal.echo("\n | The game advancement time/state has been changed.");
  game.modding.terminal.echo(" | GameStep: "+step+", Time: "+addtime+"\n");
};

say = function(text="",color=0) {
  switch (color) {
    case 0: color = "rgb(255,255,255)", cc = "White"; break;
    case 1: color = "rgb(255,55,55)", cc = "Red"; break;
    case 2: color = "rgb(55,255,55)", cc = "Green"; break;
    case 3: color = "rgb(255,55,255)", cc = "Blue"; break;
  }
  for (i=0;i<game.ships.length;i++) {
    ship = game.ships[i];
    ship.setUIComponent({id: "announceText",position: [20,75,50,25],clickable: false,visible: true,
      components: [{type: "text", position: [0,0,100,20], color: color, value: text}]
    });
  }
  if (text === "") {game.modding.terminal.echo(" | Text has been removed\n")}
  else {game.modding.terminal.echo(" | Text : "+text+", Color: "+cc+", applyed\n")}
};

set = function(who,what,crystals,stats){
  if (crystals === undefined) {
    switch (Math.trunc(what / 100)) {
      case 1: crystals = 20, stats = 11111111; break; 
      case 2: crystals = 80, stats = 22222222; break; 
      case 3: crystals = 180, stats = 33333333; break; 
      case 4: crystals = 320, stats = 44444444; break; 
      case 5: crystals = 500, stats = 55555555; break; 
      case 6: crystals = 720, stats = 66666666; break; 
      case 7: crystals = 980; break;
    }
  }
  game.findShip(who).set({type:what,crystals:crystals,stats:stats,shield:999});
  game.modding.terminal.echo("\n | Player: "+game.findShip(who).name+", id: "+who+" Has successfully been given:");
  game.modding.terminal.echo(" | Type: "+what+", Crystals: "+crystals+", Stats: "+stats+"\n");
};

game.modding.commands.qs = function() {
  NextWaveTimer = -2;
  Time = 0;
  game.modding.terminal.echo("\n | quick start\n");
};

var AddTimer = function(ship,Time,Value,ColorTimer) {
  switch(ColorTimer) {
    case 0: Color = "rgb(255,255,255)"; break; // blanc
    case 1: Color = "rgb(255,55,55)"; break; // rouge
    case 2: Color = "rgb(55,255,55)"; break; // vert
    case 3: Color = "rgb(55,55,255)"; break; // bleu
    case 4: Color = "rgb(255,55,255)"; break; // rose
    case 5: Color = "rgb(55,255,255)"; break; // bleu ciel
    case 6: Color = "rgb(255,155,55)"; break; // orange
    case 7: Color = "rgb(155,155,255)"; break; // Meg's bleu
  }
  ship.setUIComponent({id:"NextWaveTimer",position:[5,30,10,10],clickable:false,visible:true,
    components: [
      {type: "text", position: [0,0,100,50], color: Color, value: Value},
      {type: "text", position: [0,50,100,46], color: Color, value: Time}]
  });
};
// -5,-5,110,110
var AddText = function(ship,Value,Color,size=6,h=20) {
  ship.setUIComponent({id:"Text",position:[-5,-5,110,110],clickable:false,visible:true,
    components: [
      {type: "text", position: [0,h,100,size], color: Color, value:Value}]
  });
};

var tpbase = function(ship,team) { // Thanks JANNES  ;)
  if (team === 0) {
    x0 = ((Math.sqrt(2)/2)*game.options.map_size*10/2+50)*Math.cos((game.step/216000+(2/2))*Math.PI*2);
    y0 = ((Math.sqrt(2)/2)*game.options.map_size*10/2+50)*Math.sin((game.step/216000+(2/2))*Math.PI*2);
    ship.set({x:x0,y:y0,vx:0,vy:0,invulnerable:180}) ;
  }
  if (team === 1) {
    x1 = ((Math.sqrt(2)/2)*game.options.map_size*10/2+50)*Math.cos((game.step/216000+(1/2))*Math.PI*2);
    y1 = ((Math.sqrt(2)/2)*game.options.map_size*10/2+50)*Math.sin((game.step/216000+(1/2))*Math.PI*2);
    ship.set({x:x1,y:y1,vx:0,vy:0,invulnerable:180});
  }
};

        NextWaveTimer = 1;

        if (Time <= 2*60) {addcolor = 6}

          AddTimer(ship,time(Time),"Next Wave:",addcolor);
          if (WaveCount <= 1) {if (Time === 9.90*60) {ship.setUIComponent({id:"Text",visible: false})}}
          if (WaveCount === 2) {if (Time === 7.90*60) {ship.setUIComponent({id:"Text",visible: false})}}
          if (WaveCount >= 3) {if (Time === 5.90*60) {ship.setUIComponent({id:"Text",visible: false})}}
          if (Time === 2*60) {AddText(ship,Math.round(Time/60)+" minutes remains before Wave: "+WaveCount,"rgb(255,55,55)")}
          if (Time === 1.90*60) {ship.setUIComponent({id:"Text",visible: false})}
          if (Time === 0.2*60) {
            if (!this.customOptions.infinite && WaveCount >= this.customOptions.number_of_waves_for_limited) {AddText(ship,"Er..ror &#!? Errooo...","rgb(255,55,55)")}
            else {AddText(ship,"Start Hiding!","rgb(255,55,55)")}
          }
          if (Time === 0.1*60) {ship.setUIComponent({id:"Text",visible: false})}
          if (Time <= 0) {
            if (!this.customOptions.infinite && WaveCount >= this.customOptions.number_of_waves_for_limited) {
              AddText(ship,"A problem has Occurred...","rgb(255,55,55)");
              NextWaveTimer = 1.5;
              Time = 0.65*60;
            } else {
              echo("\n | Wave: "+WaveCount+"\n");
              AddText(ship,"Wave: "+WaveCount+" Started!","rgb(255,55,55)");
              sprayasteroids(this.customOptions.asteroid_number_per_wave);
              Time = 20;
              NextWaveTimer = 2;
              if (WaveCount <= this.customOptions.difficulty_change_wave) {addAliensGlobal(this.customOptions.add_alien_waves_amount,this.customOptions.add_alien_waves_code,this.customOptions.add_alien_waves_level)} 
              else {addAliensGlobal(this.customOptions.add_alien_waves_amount,this.customOptions.add_alien_waves_code,this.customOptions.add_alien_waves_level_upgrade)}
            }
          }
        }
      break;
      case 1.5:
        Time--;
        for (let ship of game.ships) {
          if (Time === 0.55*60) {ship.setUIComponent({id:"Text",visible: false})}
          if (Time === 0.50*60) {AddText(ship,"Aliens have appeared on our radar!!","rgb(255,55,55)")}
          if (Time === 0.40*60) {ship.setUIComponent({id:"Text",visible: false})}
          if (Time === 0.35*60) {AddText(ship,"Kill them to gain a special reward","rgb(255,55,55)")}
          if (Time === 0.25*60) {ship.setUIComponent({id:"Text",visible: false})}
          if (Time === 0.20*60) {AddText(ship,"Good Luck, Commanders.","rgb(255,55,55)")}
          if (Time === 0.10*60) {ship.setUIComponent({id:"Text",visible: false})}
          if (Time === 0.05*60) {AddText(ship,"Wave: "+WaveCount+" Starting..!","rgb(255,55,55)")}
        }
        if (Time === 0) {
          NextWaveTimer = 2;
          Time = 0.55*60;
        }
      break;
      case 2:
        Time --;
        for (let ship of game.ships) {
          if (!this.customOptions.infinite && WaveCount >= this.customOptions.number_of_waves_for_limited) {
            AddTimer(ship,time(Time),"End Wave:",2);
            if (Time === 0.50*60) {
              ship.setUIComponent({id:"Text",visible: false})
              sprayasteroids(this.customOptions.asteroid_number_per_wave);
              addAlienBosses(this.customOptions.alien_bosses_spawn_count);
            }
          } else {
            AddTimer(ship,time(Time),"End Wave:",1);
            if (Time === 15) {ship.setUIComponent({id:"Text",visible: false})}
          }
          if (Time < 0) {
            ship.setUIComponent({id: "NextWaveTimer",visible: false});
            NextWaveTimer = 3;
            AddText(ship,"HyperSpeed!","rgb(255,55,55)");
          }
        }
        if (Time < 0) {
          if (WaveCount > 1) {
            if (WaveCount <= this.customOptions.difficulty_change_wave) {factor = factor + this.customOptions.difficulty_multiplier_start}
            else {factor = factor + this.customOptions.difficulty_multiplier_end}
          }
          echo("\n | Wave Difficulty Factor: "+factor+"\n");
        }
      break;
      case 3:
        if (game.asteroids.length !== 0) {
          if (game.step % 40 === 0) {
            for (let ast of game.asteroids) {
              ast.set({kill:true,
                vx:(ast.vx*factor)+vxasteroids[~~(Math.random()*vxasteroids.length)],
                vy:(ast.vy*factor)+vyasteroids[~~(Math.random()*vyasteroids.length)]
              });
            }
          }
        } else {
          for (let ship of game.ships) {AddText(ship,"Wave: "+WaveCount+" Ended","rgb(55,255,55)")}
          echo("\n | Wave: "+WaveCount+" ended\n");
          Time = 0.15*60;
          NextWaveTimer = 4;
        }
      break;
      case 4:
        Time --;
        for (let ship of game.ships) {if (Time === 0.05*60) {ship.setUIComponent({id: "Text",visible: false})}}
        if (Time < 0) {
          if (!this.customOptions.infinite && WaveCount >= this.customOptions.number_of_waves_for_limited) {
            NextWaveTimer = 5;
            Time = 19;
            WaveCount ++;
            echo("\n | Next wave: "+WaveCount+"\n");
          } else {
            WaveCount ++;
            for (let ship of game.ships) {AddText(ship,"Next wave: "+WaveCount,"rgb(55,255,55)")}
            echo("\n | Next wave: "+WaveCount+"\n");
            NextWaveTimer = 0;
            ColorTimer = 0;
          }
        }
      break;
      case 5:
        Time--;
        for (let ship of game.ships) {
          if (Time === 17) {AddText(ship,"One wave remains.!","rgb(255,255,255)")}
          if (Time === 12) {ship.setUIComponent({id: "Text",visible: false})}
          if (Time === 9) {AddText(ship,"Huge wave in comming..!","rgb(255,55,55)")}
          if (Time === 4) {ship.setUIComponent({id: "Text",visible: false})}
          if (Time <= 1) {
            NextWaveTimer = 6;
            Time = 6*60;
          }
        }
      break;
      case 6:
        Time--;
        if (Time > 2*60) {addcolor = 0}
        if (Time <= 2*60) {addcolor = 6}
        if (Time <= 1*60) {addcolor = 1}
        for (let ship of game.ships) {
          if (Time === 359) {AddText(ship,"The last wave is in: "+Math.round(Time/60)+" minutes","rgb(255,255,255)")}
          if (Time === 353) {ship.setUIComponent({id: "Text",visible: false})}
          AddTimer(ship,time(Time),"Final Wave:",addcolor);
          if (Time === 2*60) {AddText(ship,Math.round(Time/60)+" minutes remains before Wave: "+WaveCount,"rgb(255,55,55)")}
          if (Time === 1.90*60) {ship.setUIComponent({id: "Text",visible: false})}
          if (Time === 0.25*60) {AddText(ship,"⚠ ️Warning asteroid rain in comming..!","rgb(255,55,55)")}
          if (Time === 0.15*60) {ship.setUIComponent({id: "Text",visible: false})}
          if (Time <= 0) {
            echo("\n | Wave: "+WaveCount+"\n");
            AddText(ship,"Final wave: "+WaveCount+" Started!","rgb(255,55,55)");
            sprayasteroids(this.customOptions.astroid_number_last_wave);
            NextWaveTimer = 7;
            Time = 0.50*60;
          }
          if (Time === 5.90*60) {ship.setUIComponent({id: "Text",visible: false})}
        }
        if (Time < 0) {
          factor = factor + (this.customOptions.difficulty_multiplier_start + this.customOptions.difficulty_multiplier_end);
          echo("\n | Wave Difficulty Factor: "+factor+"\n");
        }
      break;
      case 7:
        Time--;
        for (let ship of game.ships) {
          if (Time === 0.45*60) {ship.setUIComponent({id: "Text",visible: false})}
          AddTimer(ship,time(Time),"End Wave:",1);
        }
        if (Time <= 0) {
          for (let ship of game.ships) {AddText(ship,"HyperSpeed!","rgb(255,55,55)")}
          if (game.asteroids.length !== 0) {
            if (game.step % 40 === 0) {
              for (let ast of game.asteroids) {
                ast.set({kill:true,
                  vx:(ast.vx*2)+vxasteroids[~~(Math.random()*vxasteroids.length)],
                  vy:(ast.vy*2)+vyasteroids[~~(Math.random()*vyasteroids.length)]
                });
              }
            }
          } else {
            for (let ship of game.ships) {
              AddText(ship,"Wave: "+WaveCount+" Ended","rgb(55,255,55)");
              ship.setUIComponent({id:"NextWaveTimer",visible: false});
              NextWaveTimer = 8;
              Time = 0.65*60;
            }
            echo("\n | Wave ended: "+WaveCount+"\n");
          }
        }
      break;
      case 8:
        Time--;
        for (let ship of game.ships) {
          if (Time === 0.60*60) {ship.setUIComponent({id: "Text",visible: false})}
          if (Time === 0.55*60) {AddText(ship,"The waves are finished!","rgb(255,255,255)")}
          if (Time === 0.45*60) {ship.setUIComponent({id: "Text",visible: false})}
          if (Time === 0.40*60) {AddText(ship,"GG's everyone for surviving them, or not..","rgb(255,255,255)")}
          if (Time === 0.30*60) {ship.setUIComponent({id: "Text",visible: false})}
          if (Time === 0.25*60) {AddText(ship,"Keep fighting, the game isn't done yet!","rgb(255,255,255)")}
          if (Time === 0.15*60) {ship.setUIComponent({id: "Text",visible: false})}
          if (Time === 0.10*60) {AddText(ship,"Good luck, commanders!","rgb(255,255,255)")}
          if (Time <= 0) {
            ship.setUIComponent({id: "Text",visible: false})
            NextWaveTimer = "ended";
          }
        }
      break;
    }
  }
  if (game.step % 2000 === 0) {
    switch (NextWaveTimer) {
      case 0 || 1 || 2 || 3 || 4:
        game.modding.terminal.echo("\n");
        addEnergyZone(xx[~~(Math.random()*xx.length)],yy[~~(Math.random()*yy.length)],1,Math.random(),5);
        addEnergyZone(xx[~~(Math.random()*xx.length)],yy[~~(Math.random()*yy.length)],2,Math.random(),4);
        addEnergyZone(xx[~~(Math.random()*xx.length)],yy[~~(Math.random()*yy.length)],3,Math.random(),6);
        game.modding.terminal.echo("\n");
      break;
    }
  }
  if (game.step % 240 === 0) {
    switch (NextWaveTimer) {
      // infinite true
      case 0: addAliensCenter(this.customOptions.ac_amount,this.customOptions.ac_code,this.customOptions.ac_level); break;
      case 1: addAliensCenter(this.customOptions.ac_amount,this.customOptions.ac_code,this.customOptions.ac_level); break;
      case 4: addAliensCenter(this.customOptions.ac_amount,this.customOptions.ac_code,this.customOptions.ac_level); break;
      // infinite false
      case 6: addAliensCenter(this.customOptions.ac_amount_ew,this.customOptions.ac_code_ew,this.customOptions.ac_level_ew); break;
      case 7: addAliensCenter(this.customOptions.ac_amount_ew,this.customOptions.ac_code_ew,this.customOptions.ac_level_ew); break;
      case 8: addAliensCenter(this.customOptions.ac_amount_ew,this.customOptions.ac_code_ew,this.customOptions.ac_level_ew); break;
      case "ended": addAliensCenter(this.customOptions.ac_amount_ew,this.customOptions.ac_code_ew,this.customOptions.ac_level_ew); break;
    }
  }
  if (game.step % 25 === 0) {
    switch(loadingText) {
      case 0:
        for (let ship of game.ships) {
          AddText(ship,"Started.!","rgb(55,255,55)")
          setTimeout(() => {ship.setUIComponent({id: "Text",visible: false})}, 4500);
        }
        LoadingTime = 3;
        loadingText = 0.001;
      break;
      case 1:
        LoadingTime--;
        for (let ship of game.ships) {
          if (LoadingTime === 2) {AddText(ship,"Loading.!","rgb(55,155,55)")}
          if (LoadingTime === 1) {AddText(ship,"Loading..!","rgb(55,155,55)")}
          if (LoadingTime === 0) {
            AddText(ship,"Loading...!","rgb(55,155,55)");
            LoadingTime = 3;
          }
        }
      break;
    }
  }
};

var Adm_Button = {id: "adm_button",position: [72,0,8,4.5],clickable: true,visible: true,shortcut: "B",
  components: [{type:"box",position:[0,0,100,100],fill:"rgba(155, 155, 155, 0.40)",stroke:"rgba(155,155,155)",width:6},
    {type: "text",position:[0,20,100,60],value:"Admin [B]",color:"#FFFFFF"}]
}

var Window = {id: "window",position: [-5,-5,110,110],clickable: false,visible: true,
  components: [{type:"box",position:[this.AdminWindow.x,this.AdminWindow.y+5,40,30.5],fill:"rgba(155, 155, 155, 0.40)"},
    {type:"box",position:[this.AdminWindow.x,this.AdminWindow.y,18,5],fill:"rgba(200, 200, 200)"},
    {type:"box",position:[this.AdminWindow.x,this.AdminWindow.y+3,40,2],fill:"rgba(200, 200, 200)"},
    {type: "text",position:[-41+this.AdminWindow.x,this.AdminWindow.y,100,5],value:"Admin  Pannel",color:"#000000"}]
}

var xpg = this.AdminWindow.x;
var ypg = this.AdminWindow.y;
var AddAdminButton = function(ship,xpos,ypos,value,colorBox,ID,shortcut) {
  ship.setUIComponent({id:ID,position: [xpg+xpos,ypg+ypos,10,5.5],clickable: true,visible: true,shortcut: shortcut,
    components: [{type:"box",position:[0,0,100,100],fill:colorBox},
      {type: "text",position:[0,20,100,60],value:value+" ["+shortcut+"]",color:"#FFFFFF"}]
  })
};
var ApplySelection = function(ship,xpos,ypos,visible,value) {
  ship.setUIComponent({id:"applyall",position: [-5,-5,110,110],clickable: false,visible: visible,
    components: [{type:"box",position:[xpg+xpos,ypg+ypos,15,20],fill:"rgba(155, 155, 155, 0.40)"},
      {type: "text",position:[xpg+xpos+1.5,ypg+ypos+1,12,7],value:value,color:"#00FF00"},
      {type: "text",position:[xpg+xpos+2.5,ypg+ypos+8.4,10,10],value:"/",color:"#FFFFFF"}]
  });
  ship.setUIComponent({id:"yes",position: [xpg+xpos+1,ypg+xpos+7,4.8,8],clickable: true,visible: visible,
    components: [{type:"box",position:[0,0,100,100],fill:"rgba(55, 255, 55, 0.60)"},
      {type: "text",position:[xpos-12,ypos-8,100,100],value:"Y",color:"#FFFFFF"}]
  });
  ship.setUIComponent({id:"no",position: [xpg+xpos+9,ypg+xpos+7,4.8,8],clickable: true,visible: visible,
    components: [{type:"box",position:[0,0,100,100],fill:"rgba(255, 55, 55, 0.60)"},
      {type: "text",position:[xpos-12,ypos-8,100,100],value:"N",color:"#FFFFFF"}]
  });
};

var gpause = function() {
  for (let ship of game.ships) {
    bg(ship,true);
    ship.set({collider:false,idle:true,vx:0,vy:0});
    AddText(ship,"Game paused","rgb(55,255,55)");
    clearTimeout(this.ptm);
  }
  GamePaused = true;
  GamePlay = false;
  OldNextWaveTimer = NextWaveTimer;
  NextWaveTimer = 0.001;
  game.modding.terminal.echo("\n | Game paused.\n");
};

var gplay = function() {
  for (let ship of game.ships) {
    bg(ship,false);
    if (ship.type === spectator_ship) {ship.set({idle:false})} 
    else {ship.set({collider:true,idle:false})}
    AddText(ship,"Game resumed...","rgb(55,255,55)");
    this.ptm = setTimeout(() => {ship.setUIComponent({id:"Text",visible: false})}, 5000); // jshint ignore:line
  }
  GamePaused = false;
  GamePlay = true;
  gs(OldNextWaveTimer);
  game.modding.terminal.echo("\n | Game resumed.\n");
};

var closeAll = function(ship) {
  ship.setUIComponent({id:"window",visible:false});
  ship.setUIComponent({id:"clear_all",visible:false});
  ship.setUIComponent({id:"spectate",visible:false});
  ship.setUIComponent({id:"change_gamestep",visible:false});
  ship.setUIComponent({id:"launch_game",visible:false});
  ship.setUIComponent({id:"pause_game",visible:false});
  ship.setUIComponent({id:"play_game",visible:false});
}

var GameLaunched;
var GamePaused;
var GamePlay = true;
this.event = function(event){
  var ship = event.ship;
  switch (event.name){
    case "ui_component_clicked":
      var component = event.id;
      if (component === "adm_button") {
        if (ship.custom.Adm_Windon_open !== true) {
          ship.custom.Adm_Windon_open = true;
          ship.setUIComponent(Window);
          if (GameLaunched !== true) {AddAdminButton(ship,0,28,"Launch","rgba(100, 255, 100, 0.60)","launch_game","-")} 
          else {AddAdminButton(ship,0,28,"Launch","rgba(255, 100, 100, 0.60)","launch_game","-")}
          AddAdminButton(ship,0,7,"Clear All","rgba(100, 100, 100, 0.60)","clear_all","⚠");
          AddAdminButton(ship,30,7,"Spectate","rgba(100, 255, 100, 0.60)","spectate","-");
          if (NextWaveTimer >= 0) {
            AddAdminButton(ship,0,21,"Step","rgba(100, 255, 100, 0.60)","change_gamestep","-");
            AddAdminButton(ship,30,21,"Pause","rgba(100, 255, 100, 0.60)","pause_game","-");
            AddAdminButton(ship,30,28,"Play","rgba(100, 255, 100, 0.60)","play_game","-");
          }
        } else {
          ship.custom.Adm_Windon_open = false;
          closeAll(ship);
        }
      }
      else if (component === "clear_all") {
        //for (let alien of game.aliens) {alien.set({kill:true})}
        //for (let asteroid of game.asteroids) {asteroid.set({kill:true})}
      }
      else if (component === "spectate") {sp(ship.id)}
      else if (component === "launch_game") {
        if (GameLaunched !== true) {
          ship.custom.WhatHasBeenPressed = "launch_game";
          ApplySelection(ship,12.5,10,true,"Launch Game");
        }
      }
      else if (component === "pause_game") {if (GamePaused !== true) {gpause()}}
      else if (component === "play_game") {if (GamePlay !== true) {gplay()}}
      else if (component === "change_gamestep") {
        ship.custom.WhatHasBeenPressed = "change_gamestep";
        ApplySelection(ship,12.5,10,true,"Game Step");
      }
      else if (component === "no") {ApplySelection(ship,12.5,10,false)}
      else if (component === "yes") {
        ApplySelection(ship,12.5,10,false)
        if (ship.custom.WhatHasBeenPressed === "change_gamestep") {
          if (NextWaveTimer === 1) {gs(1,0.10)}
          if (NextWaveTimer === 6) {gs(6,0.10)}
        }
        if (ship.custom.WhatHasBeenPressed === "launch_game") {
          lg(1);
          GameLaunched = true;
          closeAll(ship);
          ship.custom.Adm_Windon_open = false;
        }
      }
    break;
  }
};

var time = function(time) {
  if (time > 0) {
    minutes = Math.floor(time/60);
    seconds = time % 60;
    if (time % 60 === 0) {minutes = time/60; seconds = "00"; return minutes.toString()+":"+seconds}
    if (seconds < 10) {seconds = "0"+seconds.toString()}
    return minutes.toString()+":"+seconds.toString();
  } else {return "0:00"}
};

var range = function(start, end) {
  var diff = end - start;
  var sign = Math.sign(diff);
  diff = Math.abs(diff) + sign;
  return Array.from({length: diff}, (v, i) => sign * i + start);
};

var Energy_Zone = {
  id: "Energy_Zone",
  obj: "https://starblast.data.neuronality.com/mods/objects/plane.obj",
  emissive: "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/TheGreatMegalodon/Dueling-Component/main/Dueling_Component/Energy_Zone.png"
};

earray = (this.customOptions.map_size*4);
var xx = [...new Array(earray)].map((j, i) => -(earray/2) + i);
var yy = [...new Array(earray)].map((j, i) => -(earray/2) + i);
var addEnergyZone = function (ID1,ID2,name,CollChanceEZ,amount) {
  if (CollChanceEZ < 1) {
    var collr1 = [10,11,20,21]; // 4 rockets pack | 2 missiles pack | 8 light mines pack | 	4 heavy mines pack
    collcode = collr1;
  }
  if (CollChanceEZ < 0.20) {
    var collr2 = [90,91]; // Energy refill | 	Shield refill
    collcode = collr2;
  }
  game.setObject({id: "Energy_Zone"+name,type: Energy_Zone,position:{x:ID1,y:ID2,z:-10},scale:{x:40,y:40,z:0},rotation:{x:Math.PI,y:0,z:0}});
  game.modding.terminal.echo("New Weapon Zone, Number: "+name+", at: x: "+ID1+" y: "+ID2+", What weapon: "+collcode);
  ID1 = [...new Array(21)].map((j, i) => ID1 - 10 + i);
  ID2 = [...new Array(21)].map((j, i) => ID2 - 10 + i);
  for (let i = 0; i < amount; i++) {
    setTimeout( () => { // jshint ignore:line
      game.addCollectible({
        code: collcode[~~(Math.random()*collcode.length)],
        x: ID1[~~(Math.random()*ID1.length)],
        y: ID2[~~(Math.random()*ID2.length)]
      });
    }, 300);
  }
  setTimeout( () => {game.removeObject("Energy_Zone"+name)}, 16000);
};

var ax = [...new Array(21)].map((j, i) => -10 + i);
var ay = [...new Array(21)].map((j, i) => -10 + i);
var cd = [15,18,23,27,31,35];
var pt = [20,23,28,25,30];
var addAliensCenter = function(amount,what,level) {
  if (game.aliens.length <= amount) {
    game.addAlien({
      level: level,
      code: what,
      points:pt[~~(Math.random()*pt.length)],
      x:ax[~~(Math.random()*ax.length)],
      y:ay[~~(Math.random()*ay.length)],
      crystal_drop:cd[~~(Math.random()*cd.length)]
    });
    game.modding.terminal.echo("\n | Alien spawned: Code: "+what+", level: "+level+"\n | points: "+pt[~~(Math.random()*pt.length)]+", crystal drop: "+cd[~~(Math.random()*cd.length)]+"\n");
  }
};

aarray = (this.customOptions.map_size*10);
var abx = [...new Array(aarray)].map((j, i) => -(this.customOptions.map_size*5) + i);
var aby = [...new Array(aarray)].map((j, i) => -(this.customOptions.map_size*5) + i);
var gcd = [40,43,47,51,56,61,65];
var gpt = [50,55,60,65,70,75,80];
var addAliensGlobal = function(amount,what,level) {
  if (game.aliens.length <= amount) {
    for (let i = 0; i < amount; i++) {
      game.addAlien({
        level: level,
        code: what,
        points:gpt[~~(Math.random()*gpt.length)],
        x:abx[~~(Math.random()*abx.length)],
        y:aby[~~(Math.random()*aby.length)],
        crystal_drop:gcd[~~(Math.random()*gcd.length)]
      });
    }
    game.modding.terminal.echo("\n | Wave aliens has arrived: Amount: "+amount+", Code: "+what+", level: "+level+"\n");
  } else {game.modding.terminal.echo("\n | Too many aliens\n")}
};
var bcd = [1000,1200,1300,1500,1700,2000];
var bpt = [100,150,200,250,300];
var addAlienBosses = function(amount) {
  for (let i = 0; i < amount; i++) {
    game.addAlien({
      level: 0,
      code: 20,
      points:bpt[~~(Math.random()*bpt.length)],
      x:abx[~~(Math.random()*abx.length)],
      y:aby[~~(Math.random()*aby.length)],
      crystal_drop:bcd[~~(Math.random()*bcd.length)],
      weapon_drop: 12
    });
  }
  game.modding.terminal.echo("\n | Alien spawned: Code: 19, level: 0 ,has arrived\n");
};

var varray = (this.customOptions.initial_velocity_asteroid*20);
var vxasteroids = [...new Array(varray)].map((j, i) => -(this.customOptions.initial_velocity_asteroid) + (i/10));
var vyasteroids = [...new Array(varray)].map((j, i) => -(this.customOptions.initial_velocity_asteroid) + (i/10));
var sasteroids = range(60,70);
var sprayasteroids = function(amount) {
  if (game.asteroids.length <= amount) {
    for (let i = 0; i < amount; i++) {
     game.addAsteroid({
        size:sasteroids[~~(Math.random()*sasteroids.length)],
        x: xx[~~(Math.random()*xx.length)], 
        y: yy[~~(Math.random()*yy.length)], 
        vx: vxasteroids[~~(Math.random()*vxasteroids.length)], 
        vy: vyasteroids[~~(Math.random()*vyasteroids.length)]
      });
      game.addAsteroid({
        size:sasteroids[~~(Math.random()*sasteroids.length)],
        x: xx[~~(Math.random()*xx.length)], 
        y: yy[~~(Math.random()*yy.length)], 
        vx: vxasteroids[~~(Math.random()*vxasteroids.length)], 
        vy: vyasteroids[~~(Math.random()*vyasteroids.length)]
      });
    }
  } else {game.modding.terminal.echo("\n | Too much asteroids\n")}
};

var rxxobj = [...new Array(6*10)].map((j, i) => -(Math.PI) + (i/10));
var ryyobj = [...new Array(6*10)].map((j, i) => -(Math.PI) + (i/10));
var rzzobj = [...new Array(6*10)].map((j, i) => -(Math.PI) + (i/10));
AddObject = function(xob,yob,GameObj) {game.setObject({id: "GameObj"+xob+yob,type: GameObj,position:{x:xob,y:yob,z:-30},scale:{x:5,y:5,z:5},rotation:{x:rxxobj[~~(Math.random()*rxxobj.length)],y:ryyobj[~~(Math.random()*ryyobj.length)],z:rzzobj[~~(Math.random()*rzzobj.length)]}})};
for (let i=0; i<20; i++) {
  AddObject(xx[~~(Math.random()*xx.length)],yy[~~(Math.random()*yy.length)],target_of_the_healing);
  AddObject(xx[~~(Math.random()*xx.length)],yy[~~(Math.random()*yy.length)],target);
}
AddObject(xx[~~(Math.random()*xx.length)],yy[~~(Math.random()*yy.length)],Alex_Ship);
